					Don Pasquale (Donizetti, Gaetano)				</h1>

<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1843
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Opera_buffa&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Opera buffa</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Operas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Operas</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="24 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Comic_operas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Comic operas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_voice&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the voice</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_mixed_chorus&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring mixed chorus</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the orchestra</a></span>; </td></tr>

<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, chorus, orchestra <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Don Pasquale (bass)<br />Dr Malatesta (baritone)<br />Ernesto (tenor)<br />Norma (soprano)<br />Carlino (bass)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Chorus</i> 
<dl><dd>sopranos, altos, tenors, basses (SATB)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i>
<dl><dd>2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones<br />timpani, percussion, harp, 2 guitars, strings </span>
